font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px;\" /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px; line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">The water impounded by these three dams of Idukki, Cheruthoni &amp; Kulamavu has formed a single reservoir spread over 60 sq.km on a height of 2300 ft above Mean Sea Level. The Idukki Dam is a double curvature arch dam constructed across Periyar River in a narrow gorge between two granite hills and is the tallest double curvature arch dam in Asia.&nbsp; Cheruthoni Dam is located 1 km west of Idukki dam. The spill way of the Idukki Reservoir is in the Cheruthony dam.&nbsp; &nbsp;Kulamavu Dam was constructed to prevent the water escape through a rivulet called Kilivally, 30 km west to Idukki Arch Dam. &nbsp;It is a 100 metres tall Masonry gravity dam. &nbsp;Construction of this Cheruthoni Dam, Idukki Arch Dam and Kulamavu Dam created an artificial lake of 60 km2 and the water stored, is used for production of electricity at the Moolamattom Power house. The power house at Moolamattom is the biggest underground power station in India and the pressure shaft is the largest in the country.</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: purple;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"color: purple;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The water used to generate electricity is taken through underground tunnels, from near the Kulamavu area, to a underground generator situated at Moolamattam..&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Kerala&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">is heavily dependent on the power generated from here and still experience power-cuts before the monsoon.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"color: purple; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Apart from the spillway (overflow) shutter at the Cheruthoni dam and the tunnels that take water to the generator, there is no way that water can be released suddenly. The dams are designed in such a way to hold water permanently till a level. When water increases above the safe level, the usual method is to increase the power generation by draining water through the tunnels and / or opening the spillway of the Cheruthoni dam.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-size: large;\"><br style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; The effects of the earthquake were felt 230 km away in Mumbai with tremors and power outages.<br />\n<br />\nLATUR EARTHQUAKE NEAR BHEED MARATHWADA---<br />\n<br />\nLatur earthquake was one of the deadliest earthquakes Maharashtra has seen till date. The earthquake struck at about 3.56 am on September 30, 1993. In the intraplate earthquake about 52 villages were destroyed, over 30,000 were injured and approximately 10,000 were killed. The earthquake left a huge hollow at Killari, which was also the epicentre, remains in place till date.<br />\n<br />\nThe 1979 MORVI DAM BURST ( rajkot , gujarat ) is in the Guinness book of world records.<br />\n<br />\nHas India ever investigated the reason for 26,000 deaths at Morvi due to induced seismicity ?<br />\n<br />\nHas India investigates the 1967 Koynanagar earthquake occurred in Maharashtra, with its epicenter, fore- and aftershocks all located near or under the Koyna Dam reservoir.<br />\n<br />\nIn dam water reservoirs, the crushing weight of the water column can significantly change the stress on an underlying fault or fracture by increasing the total stress through direct loading.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: medium;\">God has made huge NATURAL lakes in safe areas --unlike man's ARTIFICIAL DAM RESERVOIRS.</span><br />\nSignificant change in stress can lead to sudden movement along the fault or fracture, resulting in an earthquake. text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/rsyDErUWKNA/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/rsyDErUWKNA&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/rsyDErUWKNA&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is better to be united in truth <br />\nThan to be united in error. <br />\n<br />\nIt is better to tell the truth that hurts - then heals, <br />\nThan to tell a lie that heals then kills. <br />\n<br />\nIt is better to be hated for telling the truth, Than to be loved for telling a lie. </span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\nIt is better to ultimately win with the truth, Than to temporarily succeed with a lie. </span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HSvo5lXuxVY/Ts07Cc9WWkI/AAAAAAAAJDk/q3iUBcMImI4/s1600/bis056.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HSvo5lXuxVY/Ts07Cc9WWkI/AAAAAAAAJDk/q3iUBcMImI4/s640/bis056.jpg\" width=\"489\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">On 27th May 1941,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>the German battleship Bismarck was scuttled, to prevent capture by the British. Bismarck was a wondership, the largest in Europe and had the latest technology and radars.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before she sank she stopped firing at the several ships around her, and put up the cease fire flag and communicated by morse and semaphore. It made no difference.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5GxMjDqHvzc/Ts094uWdJ2I/AAAAAAAAJF8/V5xWI6D75hQ/s1600/imagesCAAQQZUZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"532\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5GxMjDqHvzc/Ts094uWdJ2I/AAAAAAAAJF8/V5xWI6D75hQ/s640/imagesCAAQQZUZ.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Out of the 2222 men on board only 114 survived, and that too just a show by the British to tell the world that they saved lives as required by law.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nearly two thousand sailors had jumped overboard in a very small area. It is a gruesome sight for the ordinary British sailor to see thousands of arms raised for help, which was ignored. The excuse given by the vindictive British command was that they were afraid of U boats in the area.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YH13g4ZG1aI/Ts07IIzlv6I/AAAAAAAAJDs/B2k8xUGmNf0/s1600/BFEW.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"628\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YH13g4ZG1aI/Ts07IIzlv6I/AAAAAAAAJDs/B2k8xUGmNf0/s640/BFEW.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Usually when a battle is won, the tradition of the British Navy was to shout a full throated and joyful \u201c Hip-Hip-Hoozzah . This time around, there&nbsp;were no hurrahs</span>.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">The common British sailor felt deeply ashamed that they had broken timeless <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>maritime traditions of picking up survivors in water, crying for help</span> . </span><span style=\"color: blue;\">Some of them cried-- just an indication that we all are human beings, not animals.</span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: purple;\">They felt terrible when they compared what transpired with the honourable conduct of Capt Langsdorff of the German battleship Graf Spee, who sank several British ships, but picked up all survivors from the water.</span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red; font-size: large;\">They could have thrown some life rafts . They could have hung some grappling nets on the ship side and stern. The ships could have streamed some mooring lines aft of them with lifebuoys and herded the men in the water in a circle.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red; font-size: large;\"><span style=\"background-color: cyan;\">So many ships, so many aircraft and seaplanes-- a very small area&nbsp;, the size of a cricket field&nbsp;with thousands of imploring , save my soul , upstretched&nbsp;arms&nbsp;.</span> </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: x-large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">What a disgrace!&nbsp; </span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: x-large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: large;\">Many British sailors developed psychological problems in their old age due to this act of dishonour -- but to be frank , it was not in the power of these pawns to help, as decisions are taken by higher ups. They knew that Churchill wanted to balance the lives lost on Hood, and also prevent further scuttling of German superships</span>. </span></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: magenta; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large; line-height: 150%;\">Since the past 20 years several eye witnesses to the dishonourable sinking of Bismarck confessed on their death beds, with sworn affidavits. This world now knows what exactly happened.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9Kpdn3NIT9Q/Ts0-BzU3SWI/AAAAAAAAJGE/zK79ytHPGwA/s1600/HA.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"243\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9Kpdn3NIT9Q/Ts0-BzU3SWI/AAAAAAAAJGE/zK79ytHPGwA/s400/HA.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It was Churchill\u2019s sweet and diabolical revenge for the loss of HMS Hood sunk by Bismarck.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Hood\u2019s magazine caught fire and she exploded into the sky.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> The Bismarck had fired a single salvo from 17 kilometers away. The elevation of her guns meant that the shells that hit the \u2018Hood\u2019 had a high trajectory and a steep angle of descent. The Hood had minimal horizontal armour and one of the shells from the Bismarck penetrated the Hood\u2019s deck and exploded in one of her magazines. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-R-ceCDMai64/Ts07ZMW3PsI/AAAAAAAAJD0/WNWdFNd2XjQ/s1600/imagesCAN2DIVZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"416\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-R-ceCDMai64/Ts07ZMW3PsI/AAAAAAAAJD0/WNWdFNd2XjQ/s640/imagesCAN2DIVZ.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A massive explosion tore the \u2018Hood\u2019 in half. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Hood had sacrificed armour for speed. Those who saw the explosion said that the bows of the \u2018Hood\u2019 were raised out of the sea before they sank. The ship sank extremely quickly and only three men (and a cat ) out of a total crew of 1,419 survived.&nbsp; Hood was the pride of the British navy.</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">After the destruction of the \u2018Hood, the Germans turned their fire onto the \u2018Prince of Wales\u2019. Her captain, Leach, decided that the best course of action was to make himself scarce. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Fleet Staff Admiral Lutjens on the Bismarck just allowed her to run away.&nbsp; However, the Bismarck had not escaped untouched by the battle. One shell had pierced two oil tanks. The damage it did to the ship was minimal but it did mean that 1000 tons of fuel was no longer available to the Bismarck. She left a oily slick in the water over her wake, which was easy to spot from the air.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fecvdutN1Sk/Ts0-LA83TiI/AAAAAAAAJGM/zDufIE7kxtM/s1600/imagesCA3JXUU9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"301\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fecvdutN1Sk/Ts0-LA83TiI/AAAAAAAAJGM/zDufIE7kxtM/s400/imagesCA3JXUU9.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then Churchill went on a lying spree. He said that the Bismarck was sunk by British ships, while Hitler insisted that the ship was scuttled just like Graf Spee, to prevent latest technology falling into enemy hands.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Zionist Jews Winston Churchill and US President FD Eisenhower pooh poohed the German claim.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ajXhJpmSJU4/Ts07fbQcs5I/AAAAAAAAJD8/CECnCKjhnqw/s1600/bis042.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ajXhJpmSJU4/Ts07fbQcs5I/AAAAAAAAJD8/CECnCKjhnqw/s640/bis042.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The wreck of <i>Bismarck</i> was discovered on 8 June 1989 by Dr. Robert Ballard , the oceanographer also responsible for finding the sunk Titanic. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He proved the British wrong. He found that Bismarck was scuttled, as she had honeycomb inner compartments . <i>Bismarck</i> rests upright at a depth of approximately 4,791 metres ( 4.7 kilometers or 3 miles deep in absolute darkness ) about 400 miles west of<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Brest France. The <i>Bismarck</i> struck an extinct underwater volcano, which rose some 1 kilometer above the surrounding abyssal plain triggering a <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>1 mile landslide. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><i>Bismarck</i> slid down the mountain, coming to a stop two-thirds down. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ballard's survey found no underwater penetrations of the ship's fully armoured citadel. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Dents on hull showed that&nbsp; most&nbsp;of the 14 inch shells fired by <i>King George V</i> bounced off the German belt armour. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sEA8g6mvRZg/Ts09TWD6tCI/AAAAAAAAJFk/FF125rJ2zX4/s1600/imagesCACLMSA9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"324\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sEA8g6mvRZg/Ts09TWD6tCI/AAAAAAAAJFk/FF125rJ2zX4/s640/imagesCACLMSA9.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ballard noted that he found no evidence of the internal implosions that occur when a hull that is not fully flooded sinks. The surrounding water, which has much greater pressure than the air in the hull, would crush the ship. Instead, Ballard points out that the hull is in relatively good condition; he states simply that \"<i>Bismarck</i> did not implode.\" <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>This suggests that <i>Bismarck's</i> compartments were flooded when the ship sank, clearly proving the scuttling theory. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Ballard had kept the exact location of the wreck a secret to prevent other divers from taking artifacts from the ship, a practice he considers a form of grave robbing\u2014already enough of injustice had been done to Bismarck. In any case it was the property of Germany as per law.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QmHotjORNK4/Ts07loN9KAI/AAAAAAAAJEE/tv4Dj75a5Ak/s1600/imagesCAFG0KJU.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"350\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QmHotjORNK4/Ts07loN9KAI/AAAAAAAAJEE/tv4Dj75a5Ak/s400/imagesCAFG0KJU.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ballard found the hull integrity to be sound, adding: \"We found a hull that appears whole and relatively undamaged by the descent and impact\" . They concluded after examining the HD underwater videos that the sole cause of sinking was due to scuttling: sabotage of engine-room valves by her crew, as claimed by German survivors and Hitler.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-nzTttQFK3KI/Ts0-U8XN5sI/AAAAAAAAJGU/vxlMA8pIcVw/s1600/wdv.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"428\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-nzTttQFK3KI/Ts0-U8XN5sI/AAAAAAAAJGU/vxlMA8pIcVw/s640/wdv.png\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In June 2001, Deep Ocean Expeditions, partnered with Woods Hole Oceanographic Institute conducted another investigation of the wreck.
